            //Collect all document ready function or handler and put it in queue where it will be executed once the Jquery is loaded
            (function (w, d, u) {
                w.readyQ = [];
                w.bindReadyQ = [];
                w.loadQ = [];
                w.bindLoadQ = [];

                function p(x, y) {
                    if (x == "ready") {
                        w.bindReadyQ.push(y);
                    } else {
                        w.readyQ.push(x);
                    }
                };
                function q(x, y) {
                    if (x == "load") {
                        w.bindLoadQ.push(y);
                    } else {
                        w.loadQ.push(x);
                    }
                };
                var a = {
                    ready: p,
                    bind: p
                };
                var b = {
                    load: q,
                    bind: q
                };
                w.$ = w.jQuery = function (f) {
                    if (f === d || f === u) {
                        return a
                    }
                    else if (f === w) {
                        return b
                    } else {
                        p(f)
                    }
                }
            })(window, document)
        </script>

    <script type="text/javascript">
        //Needed for defer loaded jquery to initialize when jQuery finish loaded
        var initInterval = setInterval(function () {
            if (window.jQuery) {
                clearInterval(initInterval);
                init();
            }
        }, 20);

        function init() {
			$(document).ready(function () {

                $('li.twocolumnslink > a').on('click',
                    function (event) {
                        var parentLi = $(this).parent();

                        if ($(this).parent().attr('class').indexOf("twocolumnslink-close") != -1) {
                            parentLi.removeClass('twocolumnslink-close').addClass('twocolumnslink-open');
                        } else {
                            parentLi.removeClass('twocolumnslink-open').addClass('twocolumnslink-close');
                        }
                    });

                //Sub-Menu Mobile
                var $mlSubMenus = $('#ml-menu-container ul[data-menu*="submenu-"]');
                if ($mlSubMenus.length) {
                    $mlSubMenus.each(function () {
                        $(this).appendTo('#ml-menu-container');
                    });
                }

                //CMS Desktop
                var $cmsNavContainers = $("li[id*='main-nav-'] div.cmsNavContainer");
                if ($cmsNavContainers.length) {
                    for (var i = 0; i < $cmsNavContainers.length; i++) {
                        var $this = $($cmsNavContainers[i]);
                        $this.addClass('hidden');
                        var title = $this.find('h3').html();
                        var $childs = $this.find('ul li');

                        var $parentUl = $this.closest('ul');
                        $parentUl.append('<li class="cmsNavContainer dropdown-sub"></li>');
                        var $newCmsContainer = $parentUl.find('li.cmsNavContainer.dropdown-sub');
                        $newCmsContainer.append('<a href="#" class="dropdown-toggle" data-toggle="dropdown" role="button" aria-haspopup="true" aria-expanded="false">' + title + ' <span class="caret"></span></a>');
                        $newCmsContainer.append('<ul class="dropdown-menu dropdown-menu-sub"></ul>');
                        $newCmsContainer.find('ul').append($childs);

                        $this.remove();
                    }
                }

                //CMS Mobile
                var $mobileCmsNavContainers = $("#ml-menu-container ul.cms-submenu div.cmsNavContainer");
                if ($mobileCmsNavContainers.length) {
                    for (var i = 0; i < $mobileCmsNavContainers.length; i++) {
                        var $this = $($mobileCmsNavContainers[i]);
                        var $parentUl = $this.closest('ul.cms-submenu');

                        $this.addClass('hidden');
                        var thisTitle = $this.find('h3').html();
                        var $thisChilds = $this.find('ul li');

                        var dataMenu = $parentUl.attr('data-menu');
                        var dataSubFor = $parentUl.attr('data-sub-for');

                        $thisChilds.each(function () {
                            $(this).addClass('menu__item');
                            $(this).find('a').addClass('menu__link');
                            $(this).find('a').attr('role', 'menuitem');
                        });

                        $thisChilds.appendTo($parentUl);
                        $this.remove();

                        var $subLinkAnchor = $("#ml-menu-container a.menu__link[data-submenu='submenu-cms-" + dataSubFor + "']");
                        if ($subLinkAnchor.length) {
                            $subLinkAnchor.html(thisTitle);
                        }
                    }
                }

                $('#mobile-navbar button[aria-expanded]').on('click', function () {
                    var $this = $(this);
                    var dataTargetMenuId = $this.attr('data-target-menu');
                    var targetIsNavCollapsed = $('#' + dataTargetMenuId).hasClass('navbar-collapse');

                    if (dataTargetMenuId != null && dataTargetMenuId != '') {
                        setTimeout(function () {
                            var menuIsOpen = false;
                            if (targetIsNavCollapsed) {
                                menuIsOpen = $('#' + dataTargetMenuId).hasClass('collapse in');
                            } else {
                                menuIsOpen = $('#' + dataTargetMenuId).hasClass('menu--open');
                            }
                            $this.attr('aria-expanded', menuIsOpen);
                        }, 200);
                    }
                });

                $('#jsrHeader .dropdown').children('.dropdown-toggle').on('click', function (e) {
                    if ($(this).parent().is('.open')) {
                        $(this).attr('aria-expanded', false);
                    } else {
                        $(this).attr('aria-expanded', true);
                    }
                });
                $('#jsrHeader .dropdown-sub').children('.dropdown-toggle').on('click', function (e) {
                    if ($(this).parent().is('.open')) {
                        $(this).attr('aria-expanded', true);
                    } else {
                        $(this).attr('aria-expanded', false);
                    }
                });

                var gHNInterval = setInterval(function () {
                    if (typeof (globalHeaderNavigation) !== 'undefined') {
                        clearInterval(gHNInterval);
                        globalHeaderNavigation({"BreadcrumbAriaLabel":"Navigation Breadcrumb","InitialBreadcrumbText":"all"});
                    }
                }, 20);

            });
        }

        document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function (event) {

            var isUsingAppDomainForServices = false;
            if ('False' === 'True') {
                isUsingAppDomainForServices = true;
            }

            var hBarInterval = setInterval(function () {
                if (typeof (InitializeHeaderBarJsr) !== 'undefined') {
                    clearInterval(hBarInterval);
                    InitializeHeaderBarJsr(isUsingAppDomainForServices); // all header related script
                }
            }, 20);

        });
    </script>
<script type="text/javascript">
    function AppendLocationMostPopularJobUrl() {
        var jsCritCookie = getCookie('jsCrit');
        if (jsCritCookie === "" || jsCritCookie === null)
            return;

        var where = decodeURIComponent(getUrlVars(jsCritCookie)["where"]);
        if (where === 'undefined' || where === "")
            return;

        var list = $('.dropdown-menu .dropdown-menu-sub').children();
        $(list).each(function (index) {
            var el = $(this).children().first()
            var href = $(el).attr('href')
            if (href.indexOf("?q=") >= 0) {
                $(el).attr("href", href + "&where=" + where);
            }
        })
    }

    function getCookie(cname) {
        var name = cname + "=";
        var decodedCookie = decodeURIComponent(document.cookie);
        var ca = decodedCookie.split(';');
        for (var i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
            var c = ca[i];
            while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') {
                c = c.substring(1);
            }
            if (c.indexOf(name) == 0) {
                return c.substring(name.length, c.length);
            }
        }
        return "";
    }

    function getUrlVars(param) {
        var vars = [], hash;
        var hashes = param.split('&');
        for (var i = 0; i < hashes.length; i++) {
            hash = hashes[i].split('=');
            vars.push(hash[0]);
            vars[hash[0]] = hash[1];
        }
        return vars;
    }

</script>
<script type="text/javascript">
    window.addEventListener('load', function () {
        var lbltypehint = document.getElementById('TypeHint');
        var lbltext = "Keywords";
        if (lbltypehint != undefined && lbltypehint != null) {
            lbltypehint.setAttribute('aria-label', lbltext);
        }
    });
</script>

            if (isMobile != undefined) {
                if (isMobile.any() != null && (getCookie('jobr.splitter.cookie') === "" || getCookie('jobr.splitter.cookie') === null)) {
                    document.getElementById("jsrHeader").classList.add('showJobr');
                    document.getElementsByTagName('body')[0].classList.add('has-jobr');
                }
            }
            var isMobile = {
                Android: function () {
                    return navigator.userAgent.match(/Android/i);
                },
                BlackBerry: function () {
                    return navigator.userAgent.match(/BlackBerry/i);
                },
                iOS: function () {
                    return navigator.userAgent.match(/iPhone/i);
                },
                Opera: function () {
                    return navigator.userAgent.match(/Opera Mini/i);
                },
                Windows: function () {
                    return navigator.userAgent.match(/IEMobile/i);
                },
                any: function () {
                    return (isMobile.Android() || isMobile.BlackBerry() || isMobile.iOS() || isMobile.Opera() || isMobile.Windows());
                }
            };
    </script>

    <div role="tabpanel" class="tab-pane active" id="tab-details">
      <div id="JobBody" class="mux-card mux-job-details " data-mux="jobDetailsEventHandler mhTrackingRegistrator  jobDetails" data-container="#JobPreview" data-content="#JobDescription" data-is-cao="true" data-is-expired="false" data-job-id="96dc24c0-a6df-4897-8290-fcc13ddd94ed" data-folder-id="0" data-tracking-url="https://job-openings.monster.ca/v2/tracking/track?Js30Flow=%7B%22searchPath%22:%22%22,%22page%22:%2210%22,%22q%22:%22data+science%22,%22tm%22:%220%22,%22useLpfRootPrefix%22:true,%22stpage%22:%221%22,%22sequence%22:1%7D&amp;jobid=96dc24c0-a6df-4897-8290-fcc13ddd94ed&amp;callback=jQuery33106337970157754769_1602544279631" data-apply-btn="#PrimaryJobApply" data-email-btn="#emailFriendOpen" mux1602544279648="34">
        <div class="card-content">
      
      
      
          <div class="details-content is-preformated" id="JobDescription" tabindex="0">
            <h1>Who we are</h1><p>&nbsp;</p><p><b>Fueled by a fundamental belief that having access to financial services creates opportunity, PayPal (NASDAQ: PYPL) is committed to democratizing financial services and empowering people and businesses to join and thrive in the global economy. Our open digital payments platform gives PayPals 325 million active account holders the confidence to connect and transact in new and powerful ways, whether they are online, on a mobile device, in an app, or in person. Through a combination of technological innovation and strategic partnerships, PayPal creates better ways to manage and move money, and offers choice and flexibility when sending payments, paying or getting paid. Available in more than 200 markets around the world, the PayPal platform, including Braintree, Venmo and Xoom, enables consumers and merchants to receive money in more than 100 currencies, withdraw funds in 56 currencies and hold balances in their PayPal accounts in 25 currencies.</b></p><p><br>&nbsp;</p><p>When applying for a job you are required to create an account, if you have already created an account - click Sign In.<br><br>Creating an account will allow you to follow the progress of your applications. Our system does have some requirements that will help us process your application, below are some guidelines for creation of your account:</p><ul><li>Provide full legal First Name/Family Name  this is important for us to ensure our future hires have the right&nbsp;system set up. </li><li>Please Capitalize first letter of your First and Last Name.</li><li>Please avoid using fully capitalized text for your First and/or Last Name.</li><li>NOTE: If your name is hyphenated or has multiple capitalization, please use the same format as your government ID.</li></ul><p style="text-align%3Ainherit"></p><p style="text-align%3Aleft">Job Description Summary:</p>About Us<br>Xoom, A PayPal Service, is revolutionizing the global digital money services market by providing people with an easy, convenient, and cost-effective means of sending money worldwide. We offer a secure, fast, and inexpensive means of sending money, paying bills and topping up prepaid services across multiple digital platforms to both online and offline recipients in over 160 countries and counting.<br><br>We are looking for a Data Scientist with a positive attitude, an awesome team player, a customer champion, a rock star in preventing online fraud who has a data driven mindset that can help upscale our risk detection capabilities and provide innovative solutions based on automation, efficiency and accuracy in a high energy, fast paced, ever evolving environment.<p style="text-align%3Ainherit"></p><p style="text-align%3Aleft">Job Description:</p><p>Specific responsibilities include</p><ul><li>Works on multiple assignments simultaneously and in all areas of a standard project in the area of responsibility related to managing and mitigating Xoom financial loss caused by fraud risk (ACH returns, card chargeback and account take-over).</li><li>Accountable for own results. Reviews are mainly for consultation and sharing ideas</li><li>Focuses primarily on how to achieve overall analytic objectives of a project with speed and quality.</li><li>Suggests ideas for operational and analytical plans and objectives&nbsp;</li><li>Clear subject matter expert who can help mentor and coach junior <i>risk analysts or data scientist</i></li><li>Works independently and proficiently on multiple assignments simultaneously with speed and quality</li><li>Has working knowledge of internal and external business processes, and data, systems and flows, as well as analytic tools, processes, and methodologies to achieve the expected results with minimum supervision</li><li>Has a good understanding of Risk business trends and directions to be able to put own work in the broad business context</li><li>Identify glitches in processes and tools and develop and execute solutions to overcome general issues and obstacles with little supervision.</li><li>Learning in-depth analysis of alternatives and applying specialized knowledge</li><li>Impact of decision has moderate reach</li><li>Seeks improvement within defined tasks. Understands, evaluates, and executes improvement ideas from supervisors.&nbsp;</li><li>Build risk related variables based on fraudulent trends and insights</li></ul><p><br><br>Qualifications</p><ul><li>Masters degree, or foreign equivalent, in Statistics, Mathematics, or closely related quantitative discipline plus four (4) years of experience in the job offered or four (4) years of experience in the field of data analysis or statistical analysis</li><li>OR Bachelors degree, or foreign equivalent, in Statistics, Mathematics or closely related quantitative discipline plus six (6) years of experience in the job offered or six (6) years of progressively responsible experience in the field of data analysis or statistical analysis.</li></ul><p style="text-align%3Ainherit"></p><p style="text-align%3Aleft">Subsidiary:</p>Xoom<p style="text-align%3Ainherit"></p><p style="text-align%3Aleft">Travel Percent:</p>0<p style="text-align%3Ainherit"></p><p style="text-align%3Aleft">Primary Location:</p>San Francisco-Xoom, California, United States of America<p style="text-align%3Ainherit"></p><p style="text-align%3Ainherit"></p><p style="text-align%3Ainherit"></p><p style="text-align%3Aleft">Additional Locations:</p><p style="text-align%3Ainherit"></p><p style="text-align%3Ainherit"></p><p style="text-align%3Ainherit"></p><p style="text-align%3Ainherit"></p><p style="text-align%3Ainherit"></p><p style="text-align%3Ainherit"></p><p style="text-align%3Aleft"><b>We're a purpose-driven company whose beliefs are the foundation for how we conduct business every day. &nbsp;We hold ourselves to our One Team Behaviors which demand that we hold the highest ethical standards, to empower an open and diverse workplace, and strive to treat everyone who is touched by our business with dignity and respect. &nbsp;Our employees challenge the status quo, ask questions, and find solutions. &nbsp;We want to break down barriers to financial empowerment. &nbsp;Join us as we change the way the world defines financial freedom.</b></p><p style="text-align%3Ainherit"></p><p style="text-align%3Ainherit"></p><p style="text-align%3Ainherit"></p><p style="text-align%3Aleft">PayPal provides equal employment opportunity (EEO) to all persons regardless of age, color, national origin, citizenship status, physical or mental disability, race, religion, creed, gender, sex, pregnancy, sexual orientation, gender identity and/or expression, genetic information, marital status, status with regard to public assistance, veteran status, or any other characteristic protected by federal, state or local law. In addition, PayPal will provide reasonable accommodations for qualified individuals with disabilities. If you are unable to submit an application because of incompatible assistive technology or a disability, please contact us at <a href="mailto%3Apaypalglobaltalentacquisition%40paypal.com" target="_blank">paypalglobaltalentacquisition@paypal.com</a>.</p>

They are usually only set in response to actions made by you which amount to a request for services, such as setting your privacy preferences, logging in or filling in forms. &nbsp; &nbsp;You can set your browser to block or alert you about these cookies, but some parts of the site will not then work. </p></div></div><div class="ot-accordion-layout ot-cat-item" data-optanongroupid="C0002"><input type="checkbox" aria-expanded="false" ot-accordion="true" role="button" aria-controls="ot-desc-id-C0002" aria-labelledby="ot-header-id-C0002"><!-- Accordion header --><div class="ot-acc-hdr"><div class="ot-plus-minus"><span></span><span></span></div><h4 class="ot-cat-header" id="ot-header-id-C0002">Analytics Cookies</h4><div class="ot-tgl"><input type="checkbox" name="ot-group-id-C0002" id="ot-group-id-C0002" aria-checked="true" role="switch" class="category-switch-handler" data-optanongroupid="C0002" checked="" aria-labelledby="ot-header-id-C0002"> <label class="ot-switch" for="ot-group-id-C0002"><span class="ot-switch-nob"></span> <span class="ot-label-txt">Analytics Cookies</span></label> </div></div><!-- accordion detail --><div class="ot-acc-grpcntr ot-acc-txt"><p class="ot-acc-grpdesc ot-category-desc" id="ot-desc-id-C0002">These cookies allow us to count visits and traffic sources so we can measure and improve the performance of our site. They may be set by us or by third party providers whose services we have added to our pages. &nbsp; &nbsp;If you do not allow these cookies then some or all of these services may not function properly.</p></div></div><div class="ot-accordion-layout ot-cat-item" data-optanongroupid="C0004"><input type="checkbox" aria-expanded="false" ot-accordion="true" role="button" aria-controls="ot-desc-id-C0004" aria-labelledby="ot-header-id-C0004"><!-- Accordion header --><div class="ot-acc-hdr"><div class="ot-plus-minus"><span></span><span></span></div><h4 class="ot-cat-header" id="ot-header-id-C0004">Advertising Cookies</h4><div class="ot-tgl"><input type="checkbox" name="ot-group-id-C0004" id="ot-group-id-C0004" aria-checked="true" role="switch" class="category-switch-handler" data-optanongroupid="C0004" checked="" aria-labelledby="ot-header-id-C0004"> <label class="ot-switch" for="ot-group-id-C0004"><span class="ot-switch-nob"></span> <span class="ot-label-txt">Advertising Cookies</span></label> </div></div><!-- accordion detail --><div class="ot-acc-grpcntr ot-acc-txt"><p class="ot-acc-grpdesc ot-category-desc" id="ot-desc-id-C0004">These cookies may be set through our site by our advertising partners. They may be used by those companies to build a profile of your interests and show you relevant adverts on other sites. &nbsp; &nbsp;They are based on uniquely identifying your browser and internet device. If you do not allow these cookies, you will experience less targeted advertising.</p></div></div><div class="ot-accordion-layout ot-cat-item" data-optanongroupid="C0005"><input type="checkbox" aria-expanded="false" ot-accordion="true" role="button" aria-controls="ot-desc-id-C0005" aria-labelledby="ot-header-id-C0005"><!-- Accordion header --><div class="ot-acc-hdr"><div class="ot-plus-minus"><span></span><span></span></div><h4 class="ot-cat-header" id="ot-header-id-C0005">Social Media Cookies</h4><div class="ot-tgl"><input type="checkbox" name="ot-group-id-C0005" id="ot-group-id-C0005" aria-checked="true" role="switch" class="category-switch-handler" data-optanongroupid="C0005" checked="" aria-labelledby="ot-header-id-C0005"> <label class="ot-switch" for="ot-group-id-C0005"><span class="ot-switch-nob"></span> <span class="ot-label-txt">Social Media Cookies</span></label> </div></div><!-- accordion detail --><div class="ot-acc-grpcntr ot-acc-txt"><p class="ot-acc-grpdesc ot-category-desc" id="ot-desc-id-C0005">These cookies are set by a range of social media services that we have added to the site to enable you to share our content with your friends and networks.
